class="css-0"><p class="css-3isp13">Control access and enable settings that keep secrets out of view. Integrate with LastPass and 1Password.</p></div><h4 class="css-1miaj62">Features:</h4><div class="css-0"><p class="css-dueegq">Access control, domain restriction, secret redaction, dynamic environment variables</p></div></div></li><li class="css-1f7ssj3"><span class="block css-1a9ekss"></span><h3 class="css-1dmyte1">Opt into AI on your own terms.</h3><div class="css-paq2zi"><div class="css-0"><p class="css-3isp13">Natural language detection happens locally. AI only engages when you take action. Your data never trains public models.</p></div></div></li><li class="css-1f7ssj3"><span class="block css-1a9ekss"></span><h3 class="css-1dmyte1">Turn app analytics on or off.</h3><div class="css-paq2zi"><div class="css-0"><p class="css-3isp13">You decide whether to send your usage data and crash reports to Warp's product team.
